       <div class="article rapid-track " data-value="article_body" id="y708-article" itemref="content-header" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
        <div class="article-container" itemprop="articleBody">
         <figure class="article-figure article-hero-figure">
          <img alt="Happy ending for two-nosed dog" class="article-figure-image" itemprop="image" src="https://s.yimg.com/ea/img/-/140210/two_nose_dog_19fgakr-19fgamr.jpg"/>
          <figcaption class="article-figure-caption">
           <span class="article-caption-text">
            Happy ending for two-nosed dog
           </span>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p class="article-abstract">
          Snuffles, the Belgian shepherd who seems to have two noses, has finally found a home.
         </p>
         <p>
          The 5-month-old pup had four different owners before he ended up at the Dogs Trust Rehoming Centre in Glasgow early this year, according to the Daily Record.
         </p>
         <p>
          Dogs Trust officials say they feared the dogs strange appearance was freaking people out.
         </p>
         <p>
          Instead of his nostrils being fused together hes got some sort of split there," veterinarian Angela McAllister told the Record.
         </p>
         <p>
          She said she had never seen anything like it before and it was caused by a rare birth defect.
         </p>
         <p>
          Luckily for Snuffles his condition does not cause any health problems.
         </p>
         <p>
          He can also move both sections of his nose independently, according to the Daily Mail.
         </p>
         <p>
          Dogs Trust manager Sandra Lawton told the Record it would be a "shame" if a dog as great as Snuffles was passed over because of his looks.
         </p>
         <p>
          She described Snuffles as having a "heart of gold" and said he "is an affectionate, energetic fun-loving boy who adores his carers".
         </p>
         <p>
          The man who eventually adopted Snuffles took him for a walk first and said the pup was perfect.
         </p>
         <br/>
         <a class="article-source-ref" href="" rel="nofollow">
         </a>

{
  var YWATracker = YWA.getTracker(10001397660209);
  YWATracker.setAction(actionnumber);
  YWATracker.submit_action();

function captureScroll(cfinfo)
{

	YWATracker.setCF(25,cfinfo);

function ywafunc(action, params)
{

  if (action == 'setUrl') {
    //param will be url if action is setUrl
    YWATracker.setUrl(params);
    YWATracker.submit();

}

        template_base_path: "https://s.yimg.com/ao/i/mp/multipass-templates/20150713041115/build"
    },
    "init" : function (Y) {
        var AsyncContentLoader = new Y.AsyncContentLoader(this.config);
        AsyncContentLoader.render();
    }
});

if (typeof System !== "undefined") {
  System.y7Felibrary = { template: "https://s.yimg.com/ao/i/mp/multipass-templates/20150713041115/build" };
}

// Collate JS Dependencies
var y7jsDeps = y7jsDeps || [], y7debug = 0;

(function () {
    var i = 0,
            modsLen = y7modules.length || 0;

    y7jsDeps = ['event-base'];

    for (i; i &lt; modsLen; i += 1) {
        y7jsDeps.push(y7modules[i].module);
    }
}());


function execY7modules(Y)
{
    y7modules = y7modules || {};

    // Modules init
    Y.Array.each(y7modules, function (item, index, array) {
        item.init(Y);
    });

    y7modules = [];
}

// handle react components 
function execY7react()
{
    if (y7react !== undefined &amp;&amp; y7react.modules !== undefined &amp;&amp; Object.keys(y7react.modules).length &amp;&amp; React !== undefined) {
        
        if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
            console.log('Executing react modules');
        }

        for (var moduleIdentifier in y7react.modules) {

            if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
                console.log(moduleIdentifier);
            }

            var module = y7react.modules[moduleIdentifier];

            /* check for object to ensure we dont break any further react processing */
            if (window[module.moduleObject]) {

                React.render(
                    React.createElement(window[module.moduleObject], {
                        data: module.data,
                        config: module.config
                    }),
                    document.getElementById(module.moduleId)
                );

            }

            if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
                console.log(module);
            }

        }

        y7react = { modules: {} };

    }
}

function execY7System()
{
    // handle system components
    if (y7system !== undefined &amp;&amp; typeof(System) !== 'undefined') {
     
        System.config({
                baseURL:'https://s.yimg.com/ao/i/mp/y7-js/20150702043051/'
        });
 
        if (y7system.length) {
 
            if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
                    console.log('Executing es6 modules');
            }

            for (var x = 0; x &lt; y7system.length; x ++) {
                var module = y7system[x];

                if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
                    console.log("Loading module '" + (module.name || module.path || module) + "'");
                }

                (function(module) {
                    var path = module.path || module;

                    System.import(path).then(function(m) {
                        var constructor = Object.keys(m)[0];

                        if (!window[constructor]) {
                            window[constructor] = new m[constructor](module.config || null);
                        }
                    });

                })(module);
            }
        }
    }
}

YUI(y7data.yuiConfig).use(y7jsDeps, function (Y) {
    Y.on('domready', function() {
        execY7modules(Y);
        execY7react();
        execY7System();
    });
});
     </script>
